CommonEvent 4
Name = "MapTones"

  Page 0
    Script(["s = $game_map.effect_surface"])
    ScriptMore(["@d = 100"])
    ScriptMore(["@a = 0"])
    ScriptMore(["@b = 0"])
    ScriptMore(["while @d >= 52"])
    ScriptMore(["@d -= 2"])
    ScriptMore(["@a += rand(3)"])
    ScriptMore(["@b += rand(3)"])
    ScriptMore(["s.set_color(@a,@b,@d)"])
    ScriptMore(["wait(5)"])
    ScriptMore(["end"])
    ScriptMore(["while @d <= 98"])
    ScriptMore(["@d += 2"])
    ScriptMore(["@a -= rand(3)"])
    ScriptMore(["if @a < 0 "])
    ScriptMore(["@a = 0"])
    ScriptMore(["end"])
    ScriptMore(["@b -= rand(3)"])
    ScriptMore(["if @b < 0 "])
    ScriptMore(["@b = 0"])
    ScriptMore(["end"])
    ScriptMore(["s.set_color(@a,@b,@d)"])
    ScriptMore(["wait(5)"])
    ScriptMore(["end"])
    Empty([])
